Arvuti rakendusi näitab tihti seda ettepanekut, kuid mängijad kasutavad füüsilist tekid tavaliselt liiguvad kuvaelma korraga.\r\n\r\nVõit\r\nMängu võitis pärast kõik kaardid on kolinud oma pakkidesse.\r\nErinevad arvuti versiooni Freecelli ajalt tegelema lahendamatu mängud.\r\n\r\n\r\nAjalugu\r\nÜks vanimaid esivanemad Freecelli Kaheksa Off. In juuni 1968 väljaanne Scientific American, Martin Gardner kirjeldatud tema \"Matemaatiline Games\" veerus mängu CL Baker, mis on sarnane FreeCell, välja arvatud see, kaardid lõpp on ehitatud ülikond mitte asendusliikme värve. Gardner kirjutas: \"Mäng oli õpetatud Baker isa, kes omakorda õppinud seda inglane 1920\". See variant on nüüdsest Baker mäng. FreeCell päritolu kohta võib ulatuvad veelgi 1945 ja Skandinaavia mäng nimega Napoleon St. Helena (mitte mängu Napoleon St. Helena, tuntud ka Forty Thieves).\r\n\r\nPaul Alfille muutunud Baker mängu, tehes kaardid ehitada vastavalt vahelduvad värvid, luues FreeCell. Ta rakendas esimest arvutipõhist versioon see Tugiisik programmeerimiskeele PLATO haridus arvutisüsteemi 1978. Alfille suutis näidata kergesti äratuntav pildikesed mängukaartide on 512 * 512 mustvalge ekraan on PLATO süsteemid.\r\n\r\nSee originaal FreeCell keskkond lubatud mängude 4C10 sambad ja 1C10 rakkude lisaks standard 8 * 4 mängu. Iga variant, programmi salvestatud pingerea mängijad pikima võitnud triibud. Seal oli ka turniiri süsteem, mis võimaldas inimestel konkureerida võita raske käsitsi korjatud tehingutest. Paul Alfille kirjeldab seda alguses FreeCell keskkonnas täpsemalt intervjuu 2000. aastast.\r\n\r\n\r\nLahendamine keerukus\r\nFreeCell mäng on pidev kaartide arv. See tähendab, et konstantse ajaga, inimene või arvuti võiks loetleda kõik võimalikud käigud on andnud start konfiguratsioon ja avastada võitnud komplekti liigub või, eeldades mängu ei saa lahendada, selle puudumisest. Teha huvitav keerukus analüüsides tuleb ehitada üldistatud versioon FreeCell mängu 4 * n kaardid. See üldistatud versioon mäng on NP-täielik; see on ebatõenäoline, et algoritm tõhusam kui brute-force otsing olemas, et saab leida lahendusi suvalise üldistatud FreeCell koosseisudes.\r\n\r\nSeal on 52! (St 52 faktoriaali), või umbes 8 * 1067 erinevat tehingutest. Kuid mõned mängud on tegelikult identsed teised, sest ülikonnad määratud kaardid on meelevaldsed ega veerge saab vahetada. We were inspired by a classic interactive puzzle game for friends and family, while we were amazed by the potential of the mixed reality motion controllers, so Paint Arena was born. Many thanks to Mixed Reality Academy for the paint brush example.  \r\n\r\nInstructions:\r\nYou will need a HoloLens or a WMR immersive headset with a mixed reality motion controllers (and headphones, if not Samsung Odyssey) to enjoy this experience.\r\n\r\nThis social experience is best enjoyed in a casual standing pose. If you feel you are not at the right height after app launch, simply stand up, look forward, and say or tap \"Reset Floor Level\". \r\n\r\nYou could draw and talk to others and guess each others' drawings. If you are the first one to join, you would be assigned the drawer for the first round. You would be given a random word. Draw something to help others guess the word (without drawing any letters or digits). Once someone guesses your word correctly, a guesser will chosen at random to become the drawer. \r\n\r\nToggle \"Painting On\" to \"Paint Balling\" to start shooting paintballs and splatter the arena. Each full tank contains 100 paintballs. Every 5 seconds, you can partially refill the tank with 20 paintballs by pressing \"Refill 20 Paintballs\" button or saying the voice command \"Refill Paint Ball\". Try to move around to dodge incoming paintballs, or teleport to reposition. Score by reducing others' health bars to zero, upon which they would enter ghost mode and respawn at a random location in 10 seconds. \r\n\r\nIn Immersive headsets: Make sure you set up boundary for all experiences before you begin. While \"Painting On\", once you see your robotic right hand holding a paint brush, you can press the right hand trigger button to start drawing. While \"Paint Balling\", you can aim with your right hand controller, and press right hand trigger to shoot paintballs.\r\n\r\nOnce you see your robotic left arm holding a motion controller, you can use the touch pad to select paint color. Alternatively, you can tap \"Pick Color\" to bring up the large color wheel. \r\n\r\nIf you made a mistake, you can say \"Erase Last Stroke\" or press right hand controller grab button. You can also clear all strokes by saying \"Erase All Strokes\". \r\n\r\nTo rotate your view, point the joysticks left or right on one of the motion controllers. \r\n\r\nTo teleport, make sure the panel shows \"Teleport On\". Then point your cursor at the floor with one of the motion controllers, and hold the joystick forward until a Teleport marker appears, then release the joystick. \r\n\r\nIn HoloLens, you can use gaze, tap gesture to select options on the menu in front of you (look below chest level). You can use the same voice commands as elaborated above. While \"Painting On\", you can reach your hand out in front of you, pinch and hold while dragging the paint brush along. While \"Paint Balling\", you can aim with your gaze and air tap to shoot paintballs.\r\n\r\nBefore teleporting in HoloLens, make sure the panel shows \"Teleport On\". Then you can use your gaze to aim, and then tap to dash across the map! You could also hide the Guessing Window and the Panel if they are blocking your gazes. Remember to turn off teleport before drawing or shooting. \r\n\r\n\r\n","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, An early variant of Tic-tac-toe was played in Roman Empire, around the first century BC. It was called Terni Lapilli and instead of having any number of pieces, each player only had three, thus they had to move them around to empty spaces to keep playing. The game's grid markings have been found chalked all over Rome. However, there is some evidence to suggest that Tic-Tac-Toe could originate back to ancient Egypt. \r\nThe different names of the game are more recent. The first print reference to \"noughts and crosses\", the British name, appeared in 1864. The first print reference to a game called \"tick-tack-toe\" occurred in 1884, but referred to \"a children's game played on a slate, consisting in trying with the eyes shut to bring the pencil down on one of the numbers of a set, the number hit being scored\". \"Tic-tac-toe\" may also derive from \"tick-tack\", the name of an old version of backgammon first described in 1558. The U.S. renaming of noughts and crosses as tic-tac-toe occurred in the 20th century. \r\nWhen playing against a phone, human player is always 'O'. The player who succeeds in placing three respective marks in a horizontal, vertical, or diagonal row wins the game. Using menu button, game can be configured to play on the larger boards to connect 4 pieces, or between 2
